<p>by <a href="http://adndevblog.typepad.com/autocad/fenton-webb.html">Fenton Webb</a></p>  <p>I was recently trying to find out some detailed information about the SheetSet Manager API and I stumbled across Autodesk’s Principle Learning Content Developer, Lee Ambrosius’s Autodesk University handout document on the subject… </p>  <p>So here it is, in case it’s useful to you as it was me <img class="wlEmoticon wlEmoticon-smile" style="border-top-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-right-style: none" alt="Smile" src="/assets/image_748276.jpg" /><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: ; letter-spacing: 0pt"><font color="#000000">&#160;</font></span></p>  <h1 style="margin: 12pt 0in 6pt; line-height: normal"><span lang="EN-US"><font style="font-size: 14pt" color="#000000"><font style="font-weight: bold">Creating a reference to the Sheet Set Object</font></font></span></h1>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US"><font style="font-size: 11pt" color="#000000">The Sheet Set object allows you to access the contents of a Sheet Set (DST) file and not the Sheet Set Manager UI.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160; </span>This allows you to create new Sheet Set files, as well as the ability to modify existing Sheet Set files.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160; </span>By being able to access Sheet Set files this way, you can write custom programs that give you more flexibility than just creating a new Sheet Set from scratch or based on an existing one.</font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US"><font style="font-size: 11pt" color="#000000">The first thing that you need to know is how to reference the AcSmComponents library.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160; </span>The AcSmComponents library can be found in the Autodesk Shared folders.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160; </span>The version of the library that you need is based on the version of AutoCAD you are using. AcSmComponents18 is used for AutoCAD 2010; while AcSmComponents17 is used for AutoCAD 2007 through AutoCAD 2009.</font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><span style="mso-ansi-language: en-gb; mso-fareast-language: ja; mso-no-proof: yes"></span><span lang="EN-US"></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US"><font style="font-size: 11pt" color="#000000">Once you have referenced the library, you need to reference the namespace for the Sheet Set Manager object.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160; </span>To do this, you use the following Imports statement:</font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="background: #d9d9d9; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: normal; text-autospace: ; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-background-themecolor: background1; mso-background-themeshade: 217"><font face="Courier New"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: ; color: ; mso-bidi-font-family: &#39;Times New Roman&#39;; mso-no-proof: yes"><font color="#0000ff">Imports</font></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: ; mso-bidi-font-family: &#39;Times New Roman&#39;; mso-no-proof: yes"><font color="#000000"> ACSMCOMPONENTS18Lib</font></span></font></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: normal; text-autospace: ; mso-layout-grid-align: none"><span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes"><font style="font-size: 11pt" color="#000000">&#160;</font></span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: ; mso-bidi-font-family: &#39;Times New Roman&#39;; mso-no-proof: yes"></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US"><font style="font-size: 11pt" color="#000000">The Sheet Set Manager object is represented by the object IAcSmSheetSetMgr.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160; </span>The following code demonstrates how to reference the Sheet Set Manager object:</font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="background: #d9d9d9; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: normal; text-autospace: ; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-background-themecolor: background1; mso-background-themeshade: 217"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: ; color: ; mso-bidi-font-family: &#39;Times New Roman&#39;; mso-no-proof: yes"><font face="Courier New"><font color="#008000">' Get a reference to the Sheet Set Manager object</font></font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="background: #d9d9d9; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: 13pt; mso-background-themecolor: background1; mso-background-themeshade: 217"><font face="Courier New"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: ; color: ; line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &#39;Times New Roman&#39;; mso-no-proof: yes"><font color="#0000ff">Dim</font></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: ; letter-spacing: -0.5pt; line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: arial"><font color="#000000"> sheetSetManager </font></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: ; color: ; line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &#39;Times New Roman&#39;; mso-no-proof: yes"><font color="#0000ff">As</font></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: ; letter-spacing: -0.5pt; line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: arial"><font color="#000000"> IAcSmSheetSetMgr</font></span></font></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="background: #d9d9d9; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: 13pt; mso-background-themecolor: background1; mso-background-themeshade: 217"><font face="Courier New"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: ; letter-spacing: -0.5pt; line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: arial"><font color="#000000">sheetSetManager = </font></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: ; color: ; line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &#39;Times New Roman&#39;; mso-no-proof: yes"><font color="#0000ff">New</font></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: ; letter-spacing: -0.5pt; line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: arial"><font color="#000000"> AcSmSheetSetMgr</font></span></font></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="letter-spacing: -0.5pt; line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: arial"><font color="#000000">&#160;</font></span></p>  <h1 style="margin: 12pt 0in 6pt; line-height: normal"><span lang="EN-US"><font style="font-size: 14pt" color="#000000"><font style="font-weight: bold">Taking a look at the Sheet Set Manager Object</font></font></span></h1>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-family: arial"><font style="font-size: 11pt" color="#000000">Once you have created a reference to the Sheet Set Manager object you can then access any of the sheet set files open in AutoCAD, create a new sheet set file, or open a sheet set file.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160; </span>Below are a few of the commonly used methods available for working with the Sheet Set Manager object and sheet sets.</font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-family: arial"><font style="font-size: 11pt" color="#000000">&#160;</font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US"><font style="font-size: 11pt" color="#000000">OpenDatabase – Allows you to open an existing sheet set file.</font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US"><font style="font-size: 11pt" color="#000000">Close – Allows you to close an open sheet set file.</font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="background: #d9d9d9; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: normal; text-autospace: ; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-background-themecolor: background1; mso-background-themeshade: 217"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: ; color: ; mso-bidi-font-family: &#39;Times New Roman&#39;; mso-no-proof: yes"><font face="Courier New"><font color="#008000">' Open a Sheet Set</font></font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="background: #d9d9d9; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: normal; text-autospace: ; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-background-themecolor: background1; mso-background-themeshade: 217"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: ; mso-bidi-font-family: &#39;Times New Roman&#39;; mso-no-proof: yes"><font face="Courier New"><font color="#000000">&lt;CommandMethod(</font><span style="color: "><font color="#a31515">&quot;ADSK_OpenSheetSet&quot;</font></span><font color="#000000">)&gt; _</font></font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="background: #d9d9d9; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: normal; text-autospace: ; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-background-themecolor: background1; mso-background-themeshade: 217"><font face="Courier New"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: ; color: ; mso-bidi-font-family: &#39;Times New Roman&#39;; mso-no-proof: yes"><font color="#0000ff">Public</font></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: ; mso-bidi-font-family: &#39;Times New Roman&#39;; mso-no-proof: yes"><font color="#000000"> </font><span style="color: "><font color="#0000ff">Sub</font></span><font color="#000000"> OpenSheetSet()</font></span></font></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="background: #d9d9d9; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: normal; text-autospace: ; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-background-themecolor: background1; mso-background-themeshade: 217"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: ; mso-bidi-font-family: &#39;Times New Roman&#39;; mso-no-proof: yes"><font face="Courier New"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes"><font color="#000000">&#160;&#160;&#160; </font></span><span style="color: "><font color="#008000">' Get a reference to the Sheet Set Manager object</font></span></font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="background: #d9d9d9; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: normal; text-autospace: ; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-background-themecolor: background1; mso-background-themeshade: 217"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: ; mso-bidi-font-family: &#39;Times New Roman&#39;; mso-no-proof: yes"><font face="Courier New"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes"><font color="#000000">&#160;&#160;&#160; </font></span><span style="color: "><font color="#0000ff">Dim</font></span><font color="#000000"> sheetSetManager </font><span style="color: "><font color="#0000ff">As</font></span><font color="#000000"> IAcSmSheetSetMgr</font></font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="background: #d9d9d9; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: normal; text-autospace: ; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-background-themecolor: background1; mso-background-themeshade: 217"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: ; mso-bidi-font-family: &#39;Times New Roman&#39;; mso-no-proof: yes"><font face="Courier New"><font color="#000000"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160;&#160;&#160; </span>sheetSetManager = </font><span style="color: "><font color="#0000ff">New</font></span><font color="#000000"> AcSmSheetSetMgr</font></font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="background: #d9d9d9; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: normal; text-autospace: ; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-background-themecolor: background1; mso-background-themeshade: 217"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: ; mso-bidi-font-family: &#39;Times New Roman&#39;; mso-no-proof: yes"><font color="#000000" face="Courier New">&#160;</font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="background: #d9d9d9; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: normal; text-autospace: ; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-background-themecolor: background1; mso-background-themeshade: 217"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: ; mso-bidi-font-family: &#39;Times New Roman&#39;; mso-no-proof: yes"><font face="Courier New"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes"><font color="#000000">&#160;&#160;&#160; </font></span><span style="color: "><font color="#008000">' Open a Sheet Set file</font></span></font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="background: #d9d9d9; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: normal; text-autospace: ; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-background-themecolor: background1; mso-background-themeshade: 217"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: ; mso-bidi-font-family: &#39;Times New Roman&#39;; mso-no-proof: yes"><font face="Courier New"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes"><font color="#000000">&#160;&#160;&#160; </font></span><span style="color: "><font color="#0000ff">Dim</font></span><font color="#000000"> sheetSetDatabase </font><span style="color: "><font color="#0000ff">As</font></span><font color="#000000"> AcSmDatabase</font></font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="background: #d9d9d9; _</font></font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="background: #d9d9d9; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: normal; text-autospace: ; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-background-themecolor: background1; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US"><font style="font-size: 11pt" color="#000000">While the above example code shows the logic of creating a new sheet set and changing its properties, an exception occurs when it executes.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160; </span>The exception occurs because a sheet set must be locked it can be modified.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160; </span>The reason behind it needing to be locked is because more than one user could be working with the sheet set file at the same time.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160; </span>So prior to changing the Name and Description properties, the LockDb method must be called and then UnlockDb must be called to unlock the database once all modifications are made.</font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US"><font style="font-size: 11pt" color="#000000">The GetLockStatus method is used to return the current lock status of a sheet set database.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160; mso-bidi-font-family: &#39;Times New Roman&#39;; mso-no-proof: yes"><font color="#0000ff">End</font></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: ; line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &#39;Times New Roman&#39;; mso-no-proof: yes"><font color="#000000"> </font><span style="color: "><font color="#0000ff">Sub</font></span></span></font><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-family: arial"></span></p>  <h1 style="margin: 12pt 0in 6pt; line-height: normal"><span lang="EN-US"><font style="font-size: 14pt" color="#000000"><font style="font-weight: bold">Adding Content to the Sheet Set File</font></font></span></h1>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US"><font style="font-size: 11pt" color="#000000">It is great to be able to open a sheet set file or even create a new one from scratch, but the purpose of a sheet set is to help organize a project.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160; </span>Sheet sets use subsets to help organize the sheets/drawing layouts added to a sheet set file.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160; </span>A subset can represent a physical folder on a network or local drive, or a virtual folder that can be used to just organize the layouts in the sheet set.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160; </span>A subset is represented by the AcSmSubset object.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160; </span>A subset has the following main properties:</font></span></p>  <p class="BulletedList" style="margin: 0in 0in 6pt 0.5in; line-height: normal; text-indent: -0.25in; mso-list: l8 level1 lfo32"><font color="#000000"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: ; mso-fareast-font-family: symbol; mso-bidi-font-family: symbol"><span style="mso-list: ignore"><font face="Symbol"><font style="font-size: 11pt">·</font></font><span style="font-family: ; line-height: normal"><font face="Times New Roman"><font style="font-size: 7pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font></font></span></span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-family: arial"><font style="font-size: 11pt">Name (SetName and GetName)</font></span></font></p>  <p class="BulletedList" style="margin: 0in 0in 6pt 0.5in; line-height: normal; text-indent: -0.25in; mso-list: l8 level1 lfo32"><font color="#000000"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: ; mso-fareast-font-family: symbol; mso-bidi-font-family: symbol"><span style="mso-list: ignore"><font face="Symbol"><font style="font-size: 11pt">·</font></font><span style="font-family: ; line-height: normal"><font face="Times New Roman"><font style="font-size: 7pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font></font></span></span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-family: arial"><font style="font-size: 11pt">Description (SetDesc and GetDesc)</font></span></font></p>  <p class="BulletedList" style="margin: 0in 0in 6pt 0.5in; line-height: normal; text-indent: -0.25in; mso-list: l8 level1 lfo32"><font color="#000000"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: ; mso-fareast-font-family: symbol; mso-bidi-font-family: symbol"><span style="mso-list: ignore"><font face="Symbol"><font style="font-size: 11pt">·</font></font><span style="font-family: ; line-height: normal"><font face="Times New Roman"><font style="font-size: 7pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font></font></span></span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-family: arial"><font style="font-size: 11pt">Prompt for Template (SetPromptForDWT and GetPromptForDWT)</font></span></font></p>  <p class="BulletedList" style="margin: 0in 0in 6pt 0.5in; line-height: normal; text-indent: -0.25in; mso-list: l8 level1 lfo32"><font color="#000000"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: ; mso-fareast-font-family: symbol; mso-bidi-font-family: symbol"><span style="mso-list: ignore"><font face="Symbol"><font style="font-size: 11pt">·</font></font><span style="font-family: ; line-height: normal"><font face="Times New Roman"><font style="font-size: 7pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font></font></span></span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-family: arial"><font style="font-size: 11pt">Storage Location for New Sheets (SetNewSheetLocation and GetNewSheetLocation)</font></span></font></p>  <p class="BulletedList" style="margin: 0in 0in 6pt 0.5in; line-height: normal; text-indent: -0.25in; mso-list: l8 level1 lfo32"><font color="#000000"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: ; mso-fareast-font-family: symbol; mso-bidi-font-family: symbol"><span style="mso-list: ignore"><font face="Symbol"><font style="font-size: 11pt">·</font></font><span style="font-family: ; line-height: normal"><font face="Times New Roman"><font style="font-size: 7pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font></font></span></span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-family: arial"><font style="font-size: 11pt">Default Template for New Sheets (SetDefDwtLayout and GetDefDwtLayout)</font></span></font></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US"><font style="font-size: 11pt" color="#000000">The following method demonstrates how to create a new subset and set its properties.</font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="background: #d9d9d9; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: normal; text-autospace: ; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-background-themecolor: background1; mso-background-themeshade: 217"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: ; </span>You have already seen part of the functionality that is required to add a sheet.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160; </span>This functionality was shown in the creation of a subset.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160; </span>Sheets can exist both as part of a subset or outside of a subset.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160; </span>A sheet in a sheet set is represented by the AcSmSheet object.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160; </span>A sheet has the following main properties:</font></span></p>  <p class="BulletedList" style="margin: 0in 0in 6pt 0.5in; line-height: normal; text-indent: -0.25in; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo33"><font color="#000000"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: ; mso-fareast-font-family: symbol; mso-bidi-font-family: symbol"><span style="mso-list: ignore"><font face="Symbol"><font style="font-size: 11pt">·</font></font><span style="font-family: ; line-height: normal"><font face="Times New Roman"><font style="font-size: 7pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font></font></span></span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-family: arial"><font style="font-size: 11pt">Name (SetName and GetName)</font></span></font></p>  <p class="BulletedList" style="margin: 0in 0in 6pt 0.5in; line-height: normal; text-indent: -0.25in; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo33"><font color="#000000"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: ; mso-fareast-font-family: symbol; mso-bidi-font-family: symbol"><span style="mso-list: ignore"><font face="Symbol"><font style="font-size: 11pt">·</font></font><span style="font-family: ; line-height: normal"><font face="Times New Roman"><font style="font-size: 7pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font></font></span></span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-family: arial"><font style="font-size: 11pt">Description (SetDesc and GetDesc)</font></span></font></p>  <p class="BulletedList" style="margin: 0in 0in 6pt 0.5in; line-height: normal; text-indent: -0.25in; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo33"><font color="#000000"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: ; mso-fareast-font-family: symbol; mso-bidi-font-family: symbol"><span style="mso-list: ignore"><font face="Symbol"><font style="font-size: 11pt">·</font></font><span style="font-family: ; line-height: normal"><font face="Times New Roman"><font style="font-size: 7pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font></font></span></span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-family: arial"><font style="font-size: 11pt">Title (SetTitle and GetTitle)</font></span></font></p>  <p class="BulletedList" style="margin: 0in 0in 6pt 0.5in; line-height: normal"><font face="Times New Roman"><font style="font-size: 7pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font></font></span></span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-family: arial"><font style="font-size: 11pt">Number (SetNumber and GetNumber)</font></span></font></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US"><font style="font-size: 11pt" color="#000000">&#160;</font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US"><font style="font-size: 11pt" color="#000000">The following method demonstrates how to add a new sheet to a sheet set or subset. </font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt; </span>The process of importing a sheet versus adding a new sheet is not very different.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160; </span>To import a sheet you can use the ImportSheet or AddSheet method.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160; line-height: normal; text-autospace: ; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-background-themecolor: background1; mso-background-themeshade: 217"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: ; mso-bidi-font-family: &#39;Times New Roman&#39;; mso-no-proof: yes"><font face="Courier New"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes"><font color="#000000">&#160;&#160;&#160; </font></span><span style="color: "><font color="#008000">' Set the properties of the sheet</font></span></font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="background: #d9d9d9; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: normal; text-autospace: ; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-background-themecolor: background1; mso-background-themeshade: 217"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: ; mso-bidi-font-family: &#39;Times New Roman&#39;; mso-no-proof: yes"><font face="Courier New"><font color="#000000"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160;&#160;&#160; </span>sheet.SetDesc(description)</font></font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="background: #d9d9d9; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: normal; text-autospace: ; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-background-themecolor: background1; mso-background-themeshade: 217"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: ; mso-bidi-font-family: &#39;Times New Roman&#39;; mso-no-proof: yes"><font face="Courier New"><font color="#000000"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160;&#160;&#160; </span>sheet.SetTitle(title)</font></font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="background: #d9d9d9; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: normal; text-autospace: ; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-background-themecolor: background1; mso-background-themeshade: 217"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: ; mso-bidi-font-family: &#39;Times New Roman&#39;; mso-no-proof: yes"><font face="Courier New"><font color="#000000"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160;&#160;&#160; </span>sheet.SetNumber(number)</font></font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="background: #d9d9d9; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: normal; text-autospace: ; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-background-themecolor: background1; mso-background-themeshade: 217"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: ; mso-bidi-font-family: &#39;Times New Roman&#39;; mso-no-proof: yes"><font color="#000000" face="Courier New">&#160;</font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="background: #d9d9d9; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: normal; text-autospace: ; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-background-themecolor: background1; mso-background-themeshade: 217"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: ; mso-bidi-font-family: &#39;Times New Roman&#39;; mso-no-proof: yes"><font face="Courier New"><font color="#000000"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160;&#160;&#160; </span>ImportASheet = sheet</font></font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="background: #d9d9d9; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: 13pt; mso-background-themecolor: background1; mso-background-themeshade: 217"><font face="Courier New"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: ; color: ; line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &#39;Times New Roman&#39;; mso-no-proof: yes"><font color="#0000ff">End</font></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: ; line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &#39;Times New Roman&#39;; mso-no-proof: yes"><font color="#000000"> </font><span style="color: "><font color="#0000ff">Function</font></span></span></font></p>  <h1 style="margin: 12pt 0in 6pt; line-height: normal"><span lang="EN-US"><font style="font-size: 14pt" color="#000000"><font style="font-weight: bold">Adding Sheet Set and Sheet Properties</font></font></span></h1>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US"><font style="font-size: 11pt" color="#000000">Custom properties are a great way to ensure consistency among the values in title blocks for a project, as well as being able to track project status.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160; </span>Custom properties come in two varieties: sheet and sheet set.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160; </span>To create a custom property you need to create a reference to an AcSmCustomPropertyBag object.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160; </span>The AcSmCustomPropertyBag object is used as a container to hold any custom properties that are added to a sheet or sheet set.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160; </span>Once a reference to an AcSmCustomPropertyBag object is made, you can then create a reference to an AcSmCustomPropertyValue object; which is the actual custom property that you want to create.</font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US"><font style="font-size: 11pt" color="#000000">You use a constant to determine the type of property that will be created.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160; </span>The values that can be used are:</font></span></p>  <p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt; text-indent: -0.25in; mso-list: l14 level1 lfo34"><font color="#000000"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: ; mso-fareast-font-family: symbol; mso-bidi-font-family: symbol"><span style="mso-list: ignore"><font face="Symbol"><font style="font-size: 11pt">·</font></font><span style="font-family: ; line-height: normal"><font face="Times New Roman"><font style="font-size: 7pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font></font></span></span></span><span lang="EN-US"><font style="font-size: 11pt">CUSTOM_SHEET_PROP – Sheet property</font></span></font></p>  <p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpLast" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt; text-indent: -0.25in; mso-list: l14 level1 lfo34"><font color="#000000"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: ; mso-fareast-font-family: symbol; mso-bidi-font-family: symbol"><span style="mso-list: ignore"><font face="Symbol"><font style="font-size: 11pt">·</font></font><span style="font-family: ; line-height: normal"><font face="Times New Roman"><font style="font-size: 7pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font></font></span></span></span><span lang="EN-US"><font style="font-size: 11pt">CUSTOM_SHEETSET_PROP – Sheet set property</font></span></font></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US"><font style="font-size: 11pt" color="#000000">The following method demonstrates how to add a new custom property to a sheet or sheet set.</font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><font color="#000000"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span lang="EN-US"><font style="font-size: 11pt">Note: </font></span></b><span lang="EN-US"><font style="font-size: 11pt">It is best to create your properties first before adding any sheets programmatically, otherwise you will need to step through each sheet in the sheet set and add the property to each one manually.</font></span></font></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="background: #d9d9d9; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: normal; text-autospace: ; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-background-themecolor: background1; mso-background-themeshade: 217"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: ; color: ; mso-bidi-font-family: &#39;Times New Roman&#39;; mso-no-proof: yes"><font face="Courier New"><font color="#008000">' Set/create a custom sheet or sheet set property</font></font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="background: #d9d9d9; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: normal; text-autospace: ; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-background-themecolor: background1; mso-background-themeshade: 217"><font face="Courier New"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: ; color: ; mso-bidi-font-family: &#39;Times New Roman&#39;; mso-no-proof: yes"><font color="#0000ff">Private</font></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: ; mso-bidi-font-family: &#39;Times New Roman&#39;; mso-no-proof: yes"><font color="#000000"> </font><span style="color: "><font color="#0000ff">Sub</font></span><font color="#000000"> SetCustomProperty(</font><span style="color: "><font color="#0000ff">ByVal</font></span><font color="#000000"> owner </font><span style="color: "><font color="#0000ff">As</font></span><font color="#000000"> IAcSmPersist, _</font></span></font></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="background: #d9d9d9; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: normal; text-autospace: ; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-background-themecolor: background1; mso-background-themeshade: 217"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: ; mso-bidi-font-family: &#39;Times New Roman&#39;; mso-no-proof: yes"><font face="Courier New"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes"><font color="#000000">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font></span><span style="color: "><font color="#0000ff">ByVal</font></span><font color="#000000"> propertyName </font><span style="color: "><font color="#0000ff">As</font></span><font color="#000000"> </font><span style="color: "><font color="#0000ff">String</font></span><font color="#000000">, _</font></font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="background: #d9d9d9; mso-bidi-font-family: &#39;Times New Roman&#39;; mso-no-proof: yes"><font face="Courier New"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes"><font color="#000000">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; mso-bidi-font-family: &#39;Times New Roman&#39;; mso-no-proof: yes"><font face="Courier New"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes"><font color="#000000">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US"><font style="font-size: 11pt" color="#000000">As previously mentioned, if you create a new sheet property and you have existing sheets in the sheet set it becomes your responsibility to add the properties to the sheets.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160; </span>To add the property to all the sheets in the sheet set you need to step through each of the sheets using a loop.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160; </span>To get all the objects that are contained in the sheet set you use the GetEnumerator method and then use the GetTypeName method to determine which type of object it is you are returned.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160; </span>The following method demonstrates how to step through all the properties associated with a sheet set and make sure the ones that are flagged as a sheet property are added to each sheet in the sheet set.</font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="background: #d9d9d9; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: normal; text-autospace: ; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-background-themecolor: background1; mso-background-themeshade: 217"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: ; mso-no-proof: yes"><font color="#000000"> </font><font color="#0000ff"><span style="color: ">Sub</span></font></span></font></p>  <h1 style="margin: 12pt 0in 6pt; line-height: normal"><span lang="EN-US"><font style="font-size: 14pt" color="#000000"><font style="font-weight: bold">Working with Sheet Set Events</font></font></span></h1>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US"><font style="font-size: 11pt" color="#000000">With the lack of documentation that comes with the Sheet Set Object, it is rather a little difficult to work efficiently with events for the Sheet Set Object.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160; </span>To use an event, it must be register and then unregistered when it is no longer needed.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160; </span>The Sheet Set Object utilizes a single event handler which is designed to return a number of different constant values.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160; </span>Below is an overview of a custom class that implements the events for the Sheet Set Object and two methods used to enable and disable the event handler.</font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="background: #d9d9d9; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: normal; text-autospace: ; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-background-themecolor: background1; mso-background-themeshade: 217"><font face="Courier New"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: ; color: ; mso-bidi-font-family: &#39;Times New Roman&#39;; mso-no-proof: yes"><font color="#0000ff">Imports</font></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: ; mso-bidi-font-family: &#39;Times New Roman&#39;; mso-no-proof: yes"><font color="#000000"> ACSMCOMPONENTS18Lib</font></span></font></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="background: #d9d9d9; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: normal; text-autospace: ; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-background-themecolor: background1; mso-background-themeshade: 217"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: ; mso-bidi-font-family: &#39;Times New Roman&#39;; mso-no-proof: yes"><font color="#000000" face="Courier New">&#160;</font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="background: #d9d9d9; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: normal; text-autospace: ; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-background-themecolor: background1; mso-background-themeshade: 217"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: ; color: ; mso-bidi-font-family: &#39;Times New Roman&#39;; mso-no-proof: yes"><font face="Courier New"><font color="#008000">' Custom event handler class</font></font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="background: #d9d9d9; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: normal; text-autospace: ; mso-layout-grid-align: none; mso-background-themecolor: background1; mso-background-themeshade: 217"><font face="Courier New"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: ; mso-no-proof: yes"><font color="#000000"> </font><span style="color: "><font color="#0000ff">Sub</font></span></span></font><span lang="EN-US"></span></p>  <h1 style="margin: 12pt 0in 6pt; line-height: normal"><span lang="EN-US"><font style="font-size: 14pt" color="#000000"><font style="font-weight: bold">Where to Get More Information</font></font></span></h1>  <p class="BulletedList" style="margin: 0in 0in 6pt; line-height: normal; text-indent: 0in; tab-stops: .5in; mso-list: none"><span lang="EN-US"><font style="font-size: 11pt" color="#000000">When you first use a new feature, you will have questions.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160; </span>You need to know where to go and get answers.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160; </span>The following is a list of resources that you can use to get help:</font></span></p>  <p class="BulletedList" style="margin: 0in 0in 6pt 0.5in; line-height: normal; text-indent: -0.25in; mso-list: l22 level1 lfo9"><font color="#000000"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: ; mso-fareast-font-family: &#39;Courier New&#39;"><span style="mso-list: ignore"><font face="Courier New"><font style="font-size: 11pt">o</font></font><span style="font-family: ; line-height: normal"><font face="Times New Roman"><font style="font-size: 7pt">&#160;&#160; </font></font></span></span></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span lang="EN-US"><font style="font-size: 11pt">Help System</font></span></b><span lang="EN-US"><font style="font-size: 11pt"> – The topic <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal">Sheet Set Objects Reference</i> in the AutoCAD Help system contains the documentation related to the Sheet Set Object.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160; </span>The only downside is that the documentation leans heavily on VBA.</font></span></font></p>  <p class="BulletedList" style="margin: 0in 0in 6pt 0.5in; line-height: normal; text-indent: -0.25in; mso-list: l22 level1 lfo9"><font color="#000000"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: ; mso-fareast-font-family: &#39;Courier New&#39;"><span style="mso-list: ignore"><font face="Courier New"><font style="font-size: 11pt">o</font></font><span style="font-family: ; line-height: normal"><font face="Times New Roman"><font style="font-size: 7pt">&#160;&#160; </font></font></span></span></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span lang="EN-US"><font style="font-size: 11pt">AUGI Forums</font></span></b><span lang="EN-US"><font style="font-size: 11pt"> – The AUGI forums provide peer to peer networking where you can ask questions about virtually anything in AutoCAD and get a response from a fellow user. (<i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal"><a href="http://www.augi.com">http://www.augi.com</a> </i>)</font></span></font></p>  <p class="BulletedList" style="margin: 0in 0in 6pt 0.5in; line-height: normal; text-indent: -0.25in; mso-list: l22 level1 lfo9"><font color="#000000"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: ; mso-fareast-font-family: &#39;Courier New&#39;"><span style="mso-list: ignore"><font face="Courier New"><font style="font-size: 11pt">o</font></font><span style="font-family: ; line-height: normal"><font face="Times New Roman"><font style="font-size: 7pt">&#160;&#160; </font></font></span></span></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span lang="EN-US"><font style="font-size: 11pt">Autodesk Discussion Forums</font></span></b><span lang="EN-US"><font style="font-size: 11pt"> – The Autodesk forums provide for peer-to-peer networking and some interaction with Autodesk moderators.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160; </span>You can ask a question about anything in AutoCAD and get a response from a fellow user or Autodesk employee. (<i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal"><a href="http://www.autodesk.com/discussion">http://www.autodesk.com/discussion</a> </i>)</font></span></font></p>  <p class="BulletedList" style="margin: 0in 0in 6pt 0.5in; line-height: normal; text-indent: -0.25in; mso-list: l22 level1 lfo9"><font color="#000000"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: ; mso-fareast-font-family: &#39;Courier New&#39;"><span style="mso-list: ignore"><font face="Courier New"><font style="font-size: 11pt">o</font></font><span style="font-family: ; line-height: normal"><font face="Times New Roman"><font style="font-size: 7pt">&#160;&#160; </font></font></span></span></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span lang="EN-US"><font style="font-size: 11pt">Industry Events and Classes</font></span></b><span lang="EN-US"><font style="font-size: 11pt"> – Industry events such as AUGI CAD Camp and Autodesk University are great places to learn about new features.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160; </span>Along with industry events, you might also be able to find classes at your local technical college or Autodesk Authorized Training Center (ATC).</font></span></font></p>  <p class="BulletedList" style="margin: 0in 0in 6pt 0.5in; line-height: normal; text-indent: -0.25in; mso-list: l22 level1 lfo9"><font color="#000000"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: ; mso-fareast-font-family: &#39;Courier New&#39;"><span style="mso-list: ignore"><font face="Courier New"><font style="font-size: 11pt">o</font></font><span style="font-family: ; line-height: normal"><font face="Times New Roman"><font style="font-size: 7pt">&#160;&#160; </font></font></span></span></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span lang="EN-US"><font style="font-size: 11pt">Autodesk Developer’s Network </font></span></b><span lang="EN-US"><font style="font-size: 11pt">– If you are serious about developing applications for AutoCAD, you should consider becoming a registered Autodesk Developer.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160; </span>For information on registering as an Autodesk Developer, see <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal"><a href="http://www.autodesk.com/adn">http://www.autodesk.com/adn</a> </i>.</font></span></font></p>  <p class="BulletedList" style="margin: 0in 0in 6pt 0.5in; line-height: normal; text-indent: -0.25in; mso-list: l22 level1 lfo9"><font color="#000000"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: ; mso-fareast-font-family: &#39;Courier New&#39;"><span style="mso-list: ignore"><font face="Courier New"><font style="font-size: 11pt">o</font></font><span style="font-family: ; line-height: normal"><font face="Times New Roman"><font style="font-size: 7pt">&#160;&#160; </font></font></span></span></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span lang="EN-US"><font style="font-size: 11pt">ObjectARX SDK </font></span></b><span lang="EN-US"><font style="font-size: 11pt">– While it is named the ObjectARX SDK, it contains many samples for the Managed .NET API including using the Sheet Set Object with .NET.<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&#160; </span>For information on the ObjectARX SDK, see <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal"><a href="http://www.autodesk.com/objectarx">http://www.autodesk.com/objectarx</a> </i>.</font></span></font></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt 0.25in; line-height: 13pt"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span lang="EN-US"><font style="font-size: 11pt" color="#000000">&#160;</font></span></b></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt 0.25in; line-height: 13pt"><font color="#000000"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span lang="EN-US"><font style="font-size: 11pt">Note: </font></span></b><span lang="EN-US"><font style="font-size: 11pt">The sample files used in these handouts can be downloaded from the AU website or <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal"><a href="http://www.hyperpics.com/au2009/CP318-4">http://www.hyperpics.com/au2009/CP318-4</a> </i>.</font></span></font></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt 0.25in; line-height: 13pt"><span lang="EN-US"><font style="font-size: 11pt" color="#000000">These handouts and others can be downloaded from <i style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal"><a href="http://www.autodesk.com/auonline">http://www.autodesk.com/auonline</a> </i>.</font></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt 4.5pt;
